â”‚     â”‚                                                               â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚          After: Discovery of artifact (wonder)"               â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚                                                               â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚                                                               â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚         "Low key lighting, blue shadows, warm center         â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚                                                               â”‚  â”‚

â”‚     â”‚         "Yes, matches dark fantasy genre                      â”‚  â”‚
â”‚     â”‚          Consistent with previous cave mentions"              â”‚  â”‚

â”‚  â”‚    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,                                         â”‚    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚    video_id UUID REFERENCES videos(id),                         â”‚    â”‚

â”‚  â”‚    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'running',                        â”‚    â”‚

â”‚  â”‚  );                                                             â”‚    â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                  â”‚    â”‚
